***potentaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:potentaat.html>potentaat</a> (67971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">potentat</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">potentatus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potentaat.html>potentaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potentaten.html>potentaten</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:potentaat.html>potentaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***powwow.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a> (46634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algonquian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Algonquian languages">Algonquian</a></span></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:language.html>language</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massachusett_language" class="extiw" title="w:Massachusett language">Massachusett</a></span></span> <span class="Latn" lang="wam">pauwau</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:he.html>he</a> uses divination; <a href = vnd.unilang:he.html>he</a> practices <a href = vnd.unilang:magic.html>magic</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sorcery.html>sorcery</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narragansett_language" class="extiw" title="w:Narragansett language">Narragansett</a></span></span> <span class="Latn" lang="xnt">powwáw</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sorcerer.html>sorcerer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:shaman.html>shaman</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Algonquian" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Algonquian">Proto-Algonquian</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="alg-pro">*pawe·wa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreams.html>dreams</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:powwow.html>powwow</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">powwows</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ritual.html>ritual</a> conducted <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:native.html>Native</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:american.html>American</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shaman.html>shaman</a>.</li>

***prat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a> (37851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:talk.html>talk</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pret.html>pret</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:fun.html>fun</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:trick.html>trick</a>, prank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>prat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prat.html>pratter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">pratst</b>)
</p>

***precies.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> (329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">precis</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">precisus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praecīsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:preciezer.html>preciezer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">preciest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:exact.html>exact</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:precise.html>precise</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:accurate.html>accurate</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:careful.html>careful</a></li></ol>
